<td style="text-align: center; background: #FEA;" colspan="2"> <b><a href="/wiki/Blade_of_Grass/Transcript" title="Blade of Grass/Transcript">Read transcript</a></b>

<p>"<b>Blade of Grass</b>" is the forty-fifth episode in the fifth season of <i><a href="/wiki/Adventure_Time" title="Adventure Time">Adventure Time</a></i>. It is the one hundred&#160;and&#160;forty-ninth episode overall.
</p>
<nav id="toc" class="toc"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">[<a href="#" class="internal" id="togglelink" data-show="show" data-hide="hide">show</a>]</span></div><ol></ol></nav>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Synopsis">Synopsis</span></h2>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Finn" title="Finn">Finn</a> tries to replace his <a href="/wiki/Demon_Blood_Sword" title="Demon Blood Sword">broken sword</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Grass_Sword" title="Grass Sword">grass sword</a>, he learns the new one is cursed.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Plot">Plot</span></h2>
<p>This episode opens with Finn and <a href="/wiki/Jake" title="Jake">Jake</a> fighting off some <a href="/wiki/Slider_Guy" title="Slider Guy" class="mw-redirect">Slider Guys</a> in an old playground. Jake notices Finn is struggling with his now-broken <a href="/wiki/Demon_Blood_Sword" title="Demon Blood Sword">Demon Blood Sword</a>, and Jake has to deal with the monsters for Finn. Jake informs Finn that he needs to get a new sword but Finn has grown attached to the sword that his father gave to him. Jake then tells Finn they should go shopping for a new sword.
</p><p>Finn and Jake go through the shops and find a hut made out of grass. They find a mysterious man in there that offers them a grass sword. Finn declines but the man tells him that swords like that one were hard to come by. Finn buys it for $3 and is constantly impressed by the sword's accuracy.Â 
</p><p>Finn plays around with his new sword and becomes better at handling it. They visitÂ <a href="/wiki/Tree_Trunks_(character)" title="Tree Trunks (character)">Tree Trunks</a>, now married, and Finn cuts an apple with his new sword. This scares Tree Trunks because she thinks the cut was "too perfect." Finn and Jake ignore her warning that the sword was cursed.
</p><p>They get back to the Tree Fort and the two go to sleep. Finn has a dream in which he turns into a grass version of himself and floats off into the distance. He then takes the sword, which is now trying to attach itself to Finn, and kicks it into a river, claiming it was the worst three bucks he ever spent. He goes back home and the next morning while brushing his teeth, he notices the sword is back.
</p><p>Jake wraps his apron around the hilt of the sword and sticks a long loaf of bread on the blade, so it cannot attach itself to Finn's body, and says they need to return it. They go back to the stores and see the grass hut is gone. A group of robbers is attacking Suzy and Sue's candle shop and Finn tries to fight them off without using his sword. He fails and uses his sword to cut off all the attackers' hair, and the robbers run away in fear. The hilt of the sword wraps around Finn's hand again, and Finn and Jake ask <a href="/wiki/Choose_Goose" title="Choose Goose">Choose Goose</a> about the <a href="/wiki/Grassy_Wizard" title="Grassy Wizard">wizard</a> who sold them the sword. Choose Goose tells them he lives on top of a hill and is the only one who can lift the curse.
</p><p>Finn and Jake venture to the aforementioned hill, Finn using the sword's abilities to fight off enemies composed of grass (including a <a href="/wiki/Grass_Bear" title="Grass Bear">tardigrade</a>, of "moss piglet"). Near the top, our heroes approach the wizard's home and, after destroying all the grassy objects thrown at them with his magic and tackling him, demand that he lift the curse. The wizard laughs in Finn's face, informing him that the blade will be with him for eternity. After a short pause Finn accepts this, stating that he is "cool with that," and the sword unravels back into his arm. The wizard is dumbfounded at his reaction to the curse and gets angry as he believes that was not the way to react to a enternal curse and stares as Finn ravels and unravels the grass sword. Jake observes that Finn, having accepted the sword, can now control it. The two run down the hill away from the house after shaking off the wizard's objections to their nonchalance.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li>Even though Tree Trunks married <a href="/wiki/Mr._Pig" title="Mr. Pig">Mr. Pig</a> in the previous episode, when Finn and Jake enter <a href="/wiki/Tree_Trunks%27_house" title="Tree Trunks' house">her house</a> there is no sign of the fact that they got married, save for Tree Trunks' new wedding ring.
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cultural_references">Cultural references</span></h3>
<ul><li>On the way to Tree Trunks' house, Finn makes battle cries while swinging his sword. These cries sound similar to Link's cries fromÂ <i>The Legend of Zelda</i>Â video game series when Link swings his sword.
</li><li>The Hooligans Who Love Candles are dressed similar to the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greaser_(subculture)" class="extiw exitstitial" title="wikipedia:Greaser (subculture)">Greasers</a>, an American 1950s form of youth gang.
</li><li>The way the sword attaches itself to Finn's arm is similar to how the Venom symbiote attached itself to Peter Parker and Eddie Brock in the Spiderman comics.
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Episode_connections">Episode connections</span></h3>
<ul><li>Finn is trying to find a sword to replace his <a href="/wiki/Demon_Sword" title="Demon Sword" class="mw-redirect">Demon Sword</a> which was broken in the episode "<a href="/wiki/The_Pit" title="The Pit">The Pit</a>."
</li><li>Finn references the timeÂ <a href="/wiki/Choose_Goose" title="Choose Goose">Choose Goose</a>Â sold him theÂ <a href="/wiki/Armor_of_Zeldron" title="Armor of Zeldron">Armor of Zeldron</a>Â in "<a href="/wiki/Blood_Under_the_Skin" title="Blood Under the Skin">Blood Under the Skin</a>."
</li><li>Tree Trunks has the ring from when she got married toÂ <a href="/wiki/Mr._Pig" title="Mr. Pig">Mr. Pig</a>Â in "<a href="/wiki/Apple_Wedding" title="Apple Wedding">Apple Wedding</a>."
</li><li>Finn screams the same way he did in the episode "<a href="/wiki/Burning_Low" title="Burning Low">Burning Low</a>" three times. The first was in his dream when he was getting covered in grass, the second when he ran outside with the sword, and the third was when he saw his grass sword in the mirror.
</li><li>Finn is wearing his old pajamas and not the new ones seen in "<a href="/wiki/The_Vault" title="The Vault">The Vault</a>."
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Errors">Errors</span></h3>
<ul><li>Finn claims that Choose Goose sold him the Armor of Zeldron during the events of "<a href="/wiki/Blood_Under_the_Skin" title="Blood Under the Skin">Blood Under the Skin</a>," but in truth, he merely gave him a poem which, when deciphered, would lead to the armor's location. The poem was free, so Choose Goose technically did not sell him anything.
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Production_notes">Production notes</span></h3>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Storyline_analysis">Storyline analysis</span></h3>
<ul><li>Finn's dream in this episode foreshadows the true curse of the Grass Sword and what eventually happens to him: in the dream, the sword starts taking him over, covering him in grass from his arm to his entire body before his entire grass-covered form falls away into nothingness. This finally happens in "<a href="/wiki/Escape_from_the_Citadel" title="Escape from the Citadel">Escape from the Citadel</a>": when the sword tries to "save" him, it covers his entire arm in vegetation before it is completely ripped away from his body, taking any portion of his body covered in grass (in this case, his arm) with him.
</li></ul>
